Yesterday's Anti-Smoking Commemoration Assembly by All Circles in This City 143

Simultaneous Pledge to Reject Drugs

Yesterday (June 3rd) marked the 92nd anniversary of Lin Zexu's burning of opium. Prior to this, the Shanghai Special Municipal Party Department, the Shanghai Municipal Government, and the China National Anti-Drug Association jointly prepared and decided to hold a commemoration assembly at the City Chamber of Commerce auditorium at 10 a.m. yesterday. They also sent letters to various organs and organizations in the city, inviting them to send representatives to participate. The details of yesterday's meeting are recorded as follows:

Attendees: Representatives from over 60 organizations and individuals, including the Shanghai Special Municipal Party Department, the Shanghai Municipal Government, the Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce, the China National Anti-Drug Association, totaling over 600 people.

Assembly Staff: Presidium: Pan Gongzhan (City Party Department), Huang Jiahuai (China National Anti-Drug Association), Zhang Qun (Representative of the City Government, Chen Kecheng); Recording: Bingxun Stenography Agency, Shen Fuyang.

Chairman's Report: Chairman Pan Gongzhan delivered the opening address, stating: "Today, representatives from all circles are gathered here to hold the Anti-Smoking Commemoration Assembly. For the past eighty-odd years, the disasters suffered by China under the oppression of unequal treaties imposed by imperialists all originated from the Opium War. Ninety-two years ago, British merchants sold opium drugs in Guangzhou. In 1838, Governor-General of Liangguang, Mr. Lin Zexu, knowing the harm of opium, ordered British merchants to surrender opium, which was completely burned at Humen. This action truly represented the determination of our Chinese government and people to ban opium. If the people of the whole country could have thoroughly implemented Mr. Lin's policy at that time and strived to resist the British troops, China would not be as poor as it is today, and the people would not be as weak as they are today. Now, under the leadership of the National Government, we should strive to reject drugs according to the teachings of the late Premier Sun Yat-sen. Many representatives in this National Assembly have paid attention to the issue of drug rejection, and the final resolution was to hand it over to the National Government for proper planning. The anti-drug measures to be drafted by the National Government in the future should be based on the proposals of the National Assembly. As for the anti-drug work, it cannot be accomplished by individuals, a few people, or the government alone; it requires all the people of the country to understand the harm of opium before it can be truly effective. It is wrong to rely solely on government laws. Although the government has established very strict anti-smoking laws, what is the effect? Aren't planters still planting, peddlers still peddling, and opium smokers still smoking? Not only has it not decreased, but it has increased. Therefore, the work of eliminating drugs cannot rely solely on government laws; opium can be fundamentally eliminated. The fundamental way is to make the people aware of the harm of opium and to be able to restrain themselves, which is the most important way. In the past, when Chinese people saw opium dealers making a fortune, they all regarded opium dealing as a way to get rich and did not feel ashamed, but instead regarded it as an honorable business. Therefore, the work of rejecting drugs cannot be completed by simply holding meetings; it must be propagated to the public every day. The purpose of our meeting today is to enable the people to implement the work of rejecting drugs, not to approach opium for life, and to persuade those who used to sell and smoke opium not to sell or smoke it again in the future. This is the purpose of today's commemoration meeting." Drug Situation: Subsequently, Guo Zhenliang, representative of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, reported on the situation of smoking ban in the city in the past year (details have been seen in yesterday's newspaper). Huang Jiahuai, the director of the China National Anti-Drug Association, then reported on the anti-drug movement in the past year, briefly stating that the association has been established for nearly seven years, and has seen many difficulties and dangers. However, the association is entrusted by the people of the country and hopes to dare to forge ahead and deal with the scourge of smoke in order to seek the final victory. In the past year, the association has strived to promote the anti-drug movement, and the determination of the association to strive for progress has not been diminished due to environmental obstacles. On the occasion of the 92nd anniversary of Lin Gong Zexu's burning of opium, the association's work in the past year is briefly described as follows: (1) Anti-Drug Propaganda: The association has always regarded propaganda as the backbone of its work. Since its establishment, it has worked hard on this end at all times, and the national anti-drug organizations across the country have also based on this guideline. Both internal and external parties have advanced simultaneously, and the National Anti-Drug Movement Week and the National Tour Anti-Drug Movement are held annually. The former was held from October 1st to 7th last year, and anti-drug organizations across the country also held it together. The latter was held in the spring of this year, and the tour anti-drug movement of the association, together with anti-drug exhibits, went to various places for touring exhibitions. Recently, the Zhejiang branch also held the above two movements in eastern Zhejiang, which has greatly benefited the propaganda. (2) Anti-Drug Education: Anti-drug education is the primary work of the anti-drug movement. The association has worked hard to promote it. For example, the anti-drug exhibits compiled by the education section of the association have been sent to various places in Nanyang and Northeast for exhibitions to promote propaganda. At the same time, in order to arouse the anti-drug interest of the student community, a student anti-drug speech contest was held in November last year. In Shanghai, nine universities, more than ten middle schools, and ninety-two elementary schools participated in the competition, breaking the previous record. Recently, the association also held a national student essay competition, and places as far away as Liaoning, Guizhou, Sichuan, and Yunnan have successively signed up to join, which shows that the national academic community has felt a considerable interest in the anti-drug movement, and the number of anti-drug organizations in various places that have held separate events is even more numerous. It is estimated that there are currently thirty-eight universities and ninety-six middle schools that have signed up and submitted articles. (3) Drug Situation Survey: In addition to the usual national survey of the opium poisoning situation and the results of the smoking ban this year, the association also sent personnel to Taiwan to investigate the monopoly system, and the investigation of the drug situation of overseas Chinese in the Nanyang colonies is still ongoing. The investigation and statistics of other narcotic drugs are also in progress. (4) Supervising the Smoking Ban: The only purpose of this book is to urge the government to implement the smoking ban. Since the National Government established its capital in Nanjing and adopted the association's proposition of banning opium, the association has vowed to support this policy and promote its thoroughness. In the past year, it has done its best to expose incidents that undermine the smoking ban, such as opposing smoking in Min and Wan, and opposing special taxes in Lianghu. For the large amount of opium seized by the Shanghai Jianghai Customs several times last year, the association has also strongly requested that it be burned to show compliance with the smoking ban laws and to chill the courage of the traitorous merchants. (5) Protesting Against the Opium Public Sale Spring: The association heard from outside that the government had abandoned the policy of banning opium and adopted a public implementation system. For a time, public opinion was divided and foreign countries took notice. In order to implement its consistent proposition, the association united with the Shanghai Transshipment Corporation and the national anti-drug organizations to rise up and protest. Later, the government stated that it was not true and did not adopt this system, but the advocates are still trying their best to promote it. The association is opposing this policy of destroying the country and exterminating the race with all its strength. (6) Promoting Smoking Cessation: The fundamental key to the anti-drug movement is to establish smoking cessation hospitals in various places to benefit the compatriots who are poisoned in various places and actually save many smokers. In Shanghai, smokers often come to the association to request to be sent to the hospital to quit smoking. Most of these smokers are poor people. The association has introduced them to appropriate hospitals. However, due to the large number of people, it is difficult to cope with them. Now, it has contacted various hospitals to provide free or subsidized smoking treatment according to the status of smokers, and will send smokers to quit smoking one after another. The above-mentioned matters are the outline of the association's work in the past year, and it is mostly due to the support of all circles. If the poisonous substance of opium is not cleared up one day, the association's responsibility will not be over. In the future, it will strive for the assistance of compatriots across the country. It is deeply hoped that the people of the country will regard it as their own responsibility and jointly plan for it. This is not only the luck of the anti-drug movement, but also the luck of the party and the country.

Representative Speeches: Subsequently, Dr. Wang Jingqi gave a speech on behalf of Mr. Zhou Chucai, roughly stating that there are 131 factories manufacturing narcotic drugs in various countries around the world, and more than 1.41 million taels of morphine and heroin are imported into our country every year. The foreigners who were arrested for drug trafficking accounted for 208 in five years, and the methods of transportation are even more ingenious. The foreign soil seized by the customs was 4,755 taels in 1929 and 10,104 taels in 1930. We see the evil consequences of China being affected by foreign drugs in this way. Commentators often blame the concessions for not being recovered, but countries around the world falsely accuse us of saying that China does not ban smoking, and there is no way to ban smoking. After the Far East Investigation Team came to China, they made many inaccurate reports to the international community, and erased the advantages of China's smoking ban and said more about China's disadvantages, which is the opposite of our opinions. Imperialism regards opium as a policy to wipe out the people of the colonies they call semi-civilized or uncivilized, and constantly imports the scourge of opium, turning China into the current situation. We should certainly blame the foreigners, but for a hundred years, the people of our country who have been infected with drugs understand its harm but do not repent, and some people only seek profit and are willing to be assistants to imperialism, making themselves mentally anesthetized first. We should blame ourselves even more. Mr. Jingqi asked whether the word "sincerity" was repeatedly raised in the League of Nations. Otherwise, the world's smoking ban would go backwards. Mr. Lin knew the scourge of opium ninety-two years ago and resolutely had the Humen opium burning incident, which is why he is admired by future generations. The perseverance of this great anti-drug figure should be taken as a good example by our anti-drug comrades. If we all use the word "sincerity" to ban smoking and reject drugs, I think everyone can be successors to Mr. Lin and make China's smoking industry very clear. Finally, representatives from the two special party departments and other organizations spoke one after another, roughly hoping that compatriots across the country would unanimously join the anti-drug campaign and that the government would effectively ban smoking. Finally, the oath was taken and the meeting adjourned. It is said that anti-drug organizations across the country contacted local public groups on the same day to hold the same commemoration.

County Government Meeting: The Shanghai County Government held an anti-smoking commemoration at 10 a.m. yesterday. All staff members of the county government and various bureaus and offices attended, and the county party department also sent personnel to participate. After the meeting, etiquette was performed as usual. First, Chairman Yan Shenyu, the county magistrate, delivered the opening address. Then, Yao Fusheng, representative of the Public Security Division, reported on the situation of the smoking ban in the past year, with a total of 37 smoking cases, 355.8 taels of smokers, 187 smoking tools, 3 morphine needles, and more than 2 taels of opium bubbles and opium paste. 51 male offenders and 13 female offenders were reported. After the report, the directors of each bureau spoke successively about the harm of opium. The etiquette was completed and the meeting adjourned.

Party and Government Organs Prohibit Unauthorized Shutdowns and Strikes 144

The Shanghai Special Municipal Party Department, the Municipal Public Security Bureau, and the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau jointly issued a notice yesterday, stating: "It is hereby notified that labor and management are in the same boat and are closely related. It is even more appropriate to work together to overcome difficulties, especially in today's economic invasion. However, recent investigations have revealed that there are many disputes between labor and management due to trivial matters, and they do not apply for mediation or arbitration in accordance with the regulations of the labor-management department, and they shut down and strike suddenly. Such direct actions not only undermine industry and hinder livelihoods, but also affect public security and violate discipline. The bureau has learned from this and jointly issued a notice to reiterate the ban, urging both labor and management in the city to comply. Any disputes should first be negotiated peacefully by representatives directly. If the dispute cannot be resolved, it should be submitted to the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau for mediation in accordance with the law. If the dispute has not been resolved through mediation or arbitration, it is strictly prohibited to shut down or strike without authorization. Once verified, it will be severely punished and no leniency will be given. Please be careful of this notice."

Actual Situation of Cigarette Warehouse Coupon Fund 150

Talks by Xie Qi, Director of the Unified Tax Administration

The National News Agency reported that the market price of various cigarette warehouse coupons has recently fluctuated slightly, and those who do not know the truth outside may think that it has something to do with a part of the Guangdong cigarette tax. The reporter therefore visited Xie Qi, Director of the Unified Tax Administration of the Ministry of Finance, to inquire about the income of the cigarette unified tax and the actual situation of the guarantee of this warehouse coupon. According to Xie, the income of the central cigarette unified tax can exceed 4 million yuan per month in the autumn and winter seasons, that is, in the summer when the mildew season is worth it, the factories produce less cigarettes, and the monthly income is at least more than 3 million yuan. When the 20-year cigarette warehouse coupon was issued, although it was designated that 250,000 yuan per month would be paid from the Guangdong Province cigarette unified tax revenue as part of the fund, on the one hand, 250,000 yuan was still allocated from the unified tax balance as a provincial cooperation fund, and there was also 450,000 yuan in silver dollars to offset the likin cooperation fund. Recently, the unified tax balance is no longer allocated to Guangdong, that is, to pay for the fund, so there is no difference in the fund, and the expenditure of the tax is relatively more economical. It is estimated that the continued issuance of 19-year and 20-year cigarette warehouse coupons requires about 2.7 million yuan per month to repay the principal and interest. According to the cigarette unified tax income in May, which is currently the off-season in the mildew season, the number is still more than 3.11 million yuan, which is more than enough to repay the principal and interest. The recent drop in the price of the warehouse coupon is probably due to the lack of understanding of the original cause by foreigners. Remembering to inquire whether the unified tax warehouse coupon to be issued will affect the cigarette warehouse coupon fund, he gave a separate detailed description. The unified tax warehouse coupon is designated to use the cigarette tax balance and cotton yarn wheat flour tax as the fund, and only needs to guarantee more than 1.4 million yuan in principal and interest per month. The cotton yarn tax was only opened in February, and there are still many old stocks. These stocks were specially allowed to be exempted from the unified tax before they left the factory on April 16 to show leniency. Although there is this huge amount of tax exemption, the income in April was still more than 1.4 million yuan, and it increased to more than 1.6 million yuan in May. The actual revenue of wheat flour tax in April and May was 400,000 yuan. It is already more than enough to allocate these two items to the unified tax warehouse coupon fund.

Ziqiang Battleship Fully Completed 152

Test Drive Scheduled for the First of Next Month

The Ziqiang warship, which was ordered to be renovated by the Jiangnan Shipbuilding Bureau of the Navy, has been under construction for nearly half a year and the entire project is about to be completed. A test drive and gun test are scheduled for the first of next month. The general situation and tonnage of the ship are recorded as follows:

History of the Ship: The Ziqiang warship was originally named Jianwei and was manufactured in the Fuzhou Mawei Shipyard. It has been 42 years old. In the past, due to disrepair, the authorities regarded the project as huge and almost abandoned it. Last year, Naval Vice-Minister Chen Shaokuan urgently needed a ship for patrolling and suppressing bandits, so he made an overall plan to reform the ship and renamed it Ziqiang. In February this year, he ordered the Jiangnan Shipbuilding Bureau to rush to repair and renovate it. It has been four months since then. Because the repair and renovation project is exceptionally agile, the entire project is about to be completed.

A Glimpse of the Ship: The ship is 620 feet long, 27 feet wide, 11 feet draft, 1,000 tons of water, and has a speed of 20 nautical miles per hour. It is equipped with 12 large cannons, 3 high-altitude cannons, 2 six-pound cannons, and 8 machine guns.

Scheduled for Test Drive: The Ministry of the Navy ordered the First Fleet Command of this port yesterday to drive to Longhua on July 1 for the first test drive to clarify whether the speed and efficiency are suitable. It is also reported that Naval Vice-Minister Chen Shaokuan will personally come to Shanghai to board the ship for inspection on that day.

Municipal Public Works Bureau Encourages Private House Building Areas 154

Divided into North and South City Four Areas

Old Materials Allowed for Building Flat Houses

The Shanghai Municipal Public Works Bureau issued a notice yesterday, stating: "In order to encourage citizens to build houses, they often try to save construction costs and use old materials, which often leads to dangers. We have already issued a notice that the load-bearing parts of new houses are prohibited from using old materials without authorization. This restriction was originally to ensure public safety. However, in recent years, the cost of building materials for flat houses in undeveloped areas of the city has become increasingly expensive. The structure of flat houses is simple and not as good as buildings. There have been requests to allow the use of old materials in order to reduce costs. The bureau has reviewed the situation and decided to encourage the people to build houses, facilitate civilian rentals, reduce shantytowns, and revitalize the city. It has now designated the area west of Jumen Road and south of Xie Xu Road in the south of Shanghai, and the area north of Zhongshan North Road (formerly Sanyang Road) and west of Baoxing Road in Zhabei as pilot areas for encouraging house building. Citizens are allowed to use old materials to build low-rent flat houses for the purpose of renting. However, the load-bearing wood must be free of rot, patching, fire damage, etc., and must be completely new. The brick materials for the load-bearing walls must also be whole, with uniform size, to ensure safety. Other procedures such as applying for permits will still be handled in accordance with the provisions of the city's temporary building regulations."

National Goods Association Requests Exemption of Ramie Export Tax 155

Ramie is a Sideline Product of Farmers and Should be Treated the Same as Silk and Tea

The China National Goods Maintenance Association telegraphed the Ministry of Industry yesterday to request exemption of ramie export tax, saying: "Ministry of Industry, Minister Kong Junjian, it is reported that Liu Yufu and Zhao Shihua, representatives of the Jiangxi ramie industry, Duan Yuliang and Peng Jiqing, representatives of the Sichuan ramie industry, Zhang Guozhu, representative of the Hunan ramie industry, and Lin Shichun and Yao Chenggao, representatives of the Guangdong ramie industry, jointly signed a letter stating: 'We respectfully request that you forward the request to exempt ramie from tax in order to maintain special products and promote sales. Ramie in our country is a sideline industry of agriculture. It is woven by women with ramie as raw material. The areas of origin are mostly Jiangxi and Sichuan, followed by Hunan and Chaozhou in Guangdong, and Suzhou in Jiangsu. The total annual output is about 20 million yuan. The largest sales market is North Korea, which is no less than 1,800,000 yuan. In addition, hundreds of thousands of yuan can be sold in the north and south provinces of the country. In recent years, military affairs in the country have been frequent, and taxes and donations in various provinces have been overlapping. The Japanese in North Korea have adopted a policy of rejecting foreign goods and heavily increasing import taxes. Recently, the production area of fine cloth, which is worth more than yuan per 100 jin, is charged 72 yen, the middle grade is charged 52 yuan, and the coarse goods are also charged 34 yuan. Therefore, the annual sales in North Korea have been sharply reduced to more than half, with an annual rate of only 300,000 to 400,000 yuan. Domestic sales are affected by foreign goods and overlapping taxes, and the cost has increased, so the number of sales is also greatly reduced. If this continues, the future of the ramie business, which is a sideline industry of agriculture, will be in an unimaginable state of decline. At the current value of the government's vigorous implementation of the people's livelihood policy and the revision of the new export tax rules, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce has insight into the declining situation of domestic agriculture and commerce. On the Yangri application, in response to the requirements of the times and the commercial theories, it telegraphed the Ministry of Industry to advocate that cooked goods should be exempted from export tax according to commercial policy, and first listed ramie, which is sold in North Korea, as the first type to be exempted from tax. The far-sighted and rapid-growing vision is truly worthy of being a commercial group leading the national business community. Although the annual output of ramie, a special product of our country, is not as large as that of silk and tea, its nature is the same as that of agricultural sideline products, and it is the same as silk and tea. Now that silk and tea have been approved for tax exemption, ramie is the same. Therefore, we especially express the difficulties of agriculture and commerce, the recent decline of the ramie industry, and the urgent need to maintain the situation. We respectfully request the Ministry of Industry to submit the item of ramie to the Legislative Yuan for review and implement tax exemption in order to maintain special products and promote sales. We cannot wait to hear from you.' Since ramie is made by hand weaving and is a common item for summer use, please also allow it to be exempted from tax in the same way as handmade cloth. All farmers and merchants in the country will be infinitely grateful.' Because of the above factors, we rely on your association's leadership and advocacy of national goods, and the enthusiasm and perseverance of the whole country are admired. Therefore, we enumerate the difficult situation of the ramie business, and in addition to requesting the Ministry of Industry, we respectfully request your association to forward the request to the government for strong assistance to achieve the purpose of tax exemption. The national farmers and merchants will benefit from it.' According to this, the Standing Committee of the Association deliberated and decided to forward the report according to the situation. We respectfully request the leaders to forward the report to the Ministry of Finance for review and approval to exempt it from tax in the same way as the handmade cloth industry, so as to reduce costs and maintain industry and commerce. We cannot wait to hear from you. May we have your instructions and obey them." Wang Jiean, Wang Xingyi, and Wang Hanqi, Standing Committee Members of the China National Goods Maintenance Association, bow to you. Jiang Yin.

Goods Ordered Before the Implementation of the Export Tariff 156

Also Need to Pay Taxes According to the New Tariff Rate

The Dama Daily reported that Major-General Meilehe of the Customs Service has followed the instructions of the Ministry of Finance and notified all customs offices that all export goods must pay the full amount in accordance with the new export tariff rules issued by the government. Even those who have signed contracts with foreign countries before the implementation of the new tariff rules should also handle it in the same way and should not be allowed to reduce taxes at the time of export. According to Chinese and foreign exporters, the prices set when signing contracts are generally calculated based on the old tariff rate. Now, when delivering goods, they must pay taxes according to the new tariff rate and suffer another loss.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Requests Reduction of Export Taxes on Tung Oil and Bamboo Firecrackers and Cigarettes 157

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday received a letter from the Oil, Hemp, Firecracker, and Cigarette Industry Association requesting the transfer of a petition to the National Government for a reduction of new export taxes to benefit the export of national goods. Yesterday, it specially submitted the petition to the National Government, the Executive Yuan, and the Ministry of Finance, requesting a review and re-implementation. The summary of the telegram is as follows:

Tung Oil: To the esteemed Executive Yuan in Nanjing: On the 2nd of this month, we received a letter from the Shanghai Oil and Hemp Industry Association stating that after the Ministry of Finance announced the new export tariff regulations, the tax rate on Tung Oil was increased by a huge 2.56 times. We immediately telegraphed to request a re-evaluation of the taxable price and a lighter revision, and requested your association to forward the telegraphic draft to request a tax reduction. We read in the newspaper that your association has already presented the matter to the Ministry of Finance and strongly requested a reduction in the tax rate, which shows your great concern. We are immensely grateful. Now we have received telegram No. 6380 from the Ministry of Finance, which states: "The telegram has been received. After reviewing the new export tariff regulations, the Tung Oil tax rate was reviewed and approved by the Legislative Yuan and promulgated by decree. The Ministry is unable to comply with the request to revise the Tung Oil export tax rate to be lighter. Please be informed." The Ministry of Finance's seal. Knowing this, the matter concerns legislation, and the Ministry of Finance will not reduce the tax. The suffering of merchants cannot reach the authorities. We implore your association, since you have forwarded the matter to the Ministry of Finance, to appeal to the authorities again to find a way to provide relief so that the Tung Oil export business does not follow in the footsteps of silk and tea, etc. After arriving at the association, we found that the association stated the previous situation: Tung Oil sales abroad have been subject to American planting of Tung trees for resistance, just as Chinese tea has been invaded by Indian and Ceylon products, and the trend is only downward. The new tariff is more than 2.5 times heavier than the old tariff, which will inevitably increase costs and make it more difficult. We telegraphed to the Ministry of Finance to consider that the Tung Oil exported from our country is no longer comparable to the monopoly market of several years ago, to re-evaluate and revise the price, or to change from quantitative tax to ad valorem tax, so as to avoid excessive burden on exporters. So far, we have not received an order to reply. Now it is said that the ministry has rejected the request, and the Tung Oil exporters are suffering without the authorities' concern and relief. The heavy tax will inevitably lead to slow sales, and our country's only exported Tung Oil will fall. According to the tariff protection policy, isn't this going in the opposite direction? It is appropriate to again request your esteemed association to review and instruct the Legislative Yuan to re-examine and revise the tariff, and at the same time order the Ministry of Finance to temporarily suspend the new tax in order to maintain a lifeline for Tung Oil."

Firecrackers: To the esteemed National Government Ministry of Finance: On May 30, we received a letter from the Firecracker Industry Association of this city stating that the new export tariff regulations promulgated by the National Government tax firecrackers at 1.2 taels per picul, an increase of 7 mace over the original tax rate, which is shocking. The firecracker is purely a handicraft product, and its raw materials, paper and sulfur, have already been taxed. According to the principle of one tax per item, the firecrackers made of this paper and sulfur should be exempted from tax. 1. Most of the sales markets for firecrackers are in Mumbai, Annam, and various ports in Southeast Asia. In order to promote export trade, it should be requested to be tax-free. 2. The number of workers and merchants who live directly and indirectly on firecrackers is no less than several million. In order to maintain the development of their livelihoods, it should be requested to be tax-free. 3. This letter is sent to respectfully request your review and transfer it to the government to follow the precedents of tea and silk to allow tax exemption in order to facilitate development. Upon arrival at the association, it was found that the firecracker industry is related to the livelihood of manual workers. Traditionally, the only place where exports have been sold abroad is Annam, which is worth more than 6 million francs (according to French statistics in 1925). Together with tea and medicines, it is an important export item of China. The association telegraphed to your government on May 7 of this year, stating that the export tax on firecrackers should not be increased. If the newly revised tax rate passed by the Legislative Yuan is indeed higher than before for this export tax, it should be reviewed, revised, and promulgated again. Based on the previous letter, it is appropriate to telegraph again for review and approval as requested.

Cigarettes: (Above omitted) On May 30, we received a letter from the Chinese Cigarette Factory Association (reported in the previous newspaper), specially sent to your association to quickly submit it to the Ministry of Industry and to consider the difficulties of merchants and to provide protection, and to forward it to the National Government to promote the purpose of national products and to temporarily suspend the implementation of the cigarette export tax. Upon arrival at the association, it was found that cigarettes are indeed a consumable product sold domestically. Promoting sales abroad is a manufactured product rather than a raw material. From the perspective of international trade, it should still be encouraged. Therefore, according to the method of imitating foreign goods with machines, the export tax is exempted because it is shipped abroad. Although the newly revised export tariff regulations include machine-made cotton yarn and imitation cigarettes in the tax items, the telegram from the Customs Administration to the Federation of Chinese Yarn Factories stated that the collection and exemption of tariffs on cotton yarn and cotton cloth exported to foreign countries will still be handled according to the existing regulations. That is, the established case of tax exemption for machine-made imitation foreign goods exported abroad will not be changed due to the newly revised export tariff regulations. The machine-made cigarettes are subject to the same rule. It is appropriate to telegraph to clarify the situation in order to reassure merchants. It is for the public good. Respectfully from the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce.

Qian Chengxu's Talk After Returning to Shanghai 158

Recent Situation of Beining Railway and Kailuan Mining

The Beining Railway Bureau and the Kailuan Mining Bureau had a misunderstanding due to issues such as liquidation, train suspension, and delayed freight charges, which caused a dispute that lasted for more than two months and remained unresolved. In view of the environmental needs, the China General Federation of Industry and the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce specially appointed Qian Chengxu as a representative to go to Beiping to mediate with the Kailuan authorities. Yesterday, he returned to Shanghai and said that his mission was not disgraced, and there was no problem with the recovery of coal transportation. The reporter asked Mr. Qian about the reasons for going to Beiping and the process of mediation. Mr. Qian replied that around 1920 and 1930, domestic wars were not over. Kailuan Mining, because of its foreign investment, was not devastated by the war. Users in various places were happy to trade with it because it could provide supplies on time, and they did not prepare large amounts of coal in advance. In March of this year, coal arrived in Shanghai and felt a shortage. The impact was that the market for the coal industry was affected by the inability to adjust supply and demand. Japanese coal took the opportunity to flood the market and could not be contained. At that time, users and the mining bureau had a supply contract, but in fact, after investigation, the sales office had no coal to deliver, and users were unable to purchase from other places due to the high price of coal. They were afraid that a coal shortage would occur when the supply was not available. My mission to Beiping was to promote the recovery of Kailuan in order to have fundamental relief. As for the mediation process, I started from Shanghai on May 12 and presented the general situation to the relevant departments in Beijing and Tianjin. The Ministry of Industry sent Director Lao Shuzhuang of the Labor Bureau and Director Hu Boyuan of the Mining Administration to investigate. On the 14th, I went to Tianjin to meet with Hu Ruoyu, the director of Kailuan Mining, who agreed to take responsibility for mediation. Soon after, Deputy Commander Zhang of the capital sent a telegram to urge him, and Minister Wang of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs also came forward to mediate. At this time, the attitude of both parties was likely to approach. I will not talk about the official language. At that time, I also proposed conditions to both parties in my position as a mediator: one party would restore the Kailuan coal transportation situation, and the other party would provide 1 million yuan in cash in the name of the industrial and commercial groups as collateral for the Kailuan liquidation account. The Kailuan authorities agreed to give serious consideration to this, but after May 20, both parties began direct negotiations. By the time I returned to the south, all outstanding cases had a predetermined solution plan, and the formalities could be completed after both parties signed. At this point, the reporter asked Mr. Qian about the recent observations of coal use in North China and the business situation of Kailuan. Mr. Qian replied that the source of coal used in North China is very broad. For example, the mines of Kailuan in Hebei Province, Jingxing in Lincheng, Beipiao in Liaoning Province, Zhongkang in Henan Province, Baogao and Datong in Shanxi Province, and Zhongxing and Ludong in Shandong Province have all occupied a considerable position today. The users do not feel a shortage of coal due to the Kailuan problem. In short, the regional status of the coal mine is that more local products are sold locally, which is the convenience of the time and place, which is different from the situation in South China. As for the Kailuan business policy, I observed that since 1921, one party has adopted a huge production policy, and the other party has organized a powerful sales machine. Therefore, it can supply the market with low-priced goods and can directly sell goods to users to eliminate the heavy rebate of middlemen. In addition, the former Jingfeng Railway Bureau's successive foreign car affairs general camps were also British, and their nationalities were the same, and they could contact each other in many ways to obtain convenience. The daily output of coal was only about 8,000 tons a day ten years ago, but now it has jumped to more than 60,000 tons, occupying the first position in the domestic coal mines. However, according to the current situation, the Beining Railway Bureau's car affairs are now managed by Chinese, and in addition to this dispute, foreigners have understood their own environment. As a result, it may abandon its active policy and adopt a tight policy.

Dissolution of the Seamen's Association 159

The Shanghai Seamen's Industrial Federation is located on Qiujiang Road in northern Shanghai and is the general organization of seamen from various ships. There is also a Shanghai branch in the southern city. In addition to the small amount of membership fees, the association's funding is provided by the Central Party Headquarters with a monthly allocation of more than 2,000 yuan as the association's operating expenses. In April of this year, the association planned to convene a national seamen's representative meeting to report to the Central Party Headquarters. The approval was given that the association must reorganize according to the new organization, and the full representative meeting was temporarily postponed, so it was not implemented. Now the association must implement reorganization and has automatically dissolved. All internal committee members have also left the association. All official documents, equipment, and other items will be temporarily taken over by the Shanghai Municipal Party Headquarters. Before the takeover, they will be sealed and police from the Public Security Bureau will be stationed to guard them.

The situation yesterday is recorded as follows:

Preventing Work: Yesterday, the striking workers found that Youwen Bookbinding in Hongxingfang, Hongxing Road, Zhabei, was working as usual. At about 8:00 am, they went to prevent it. Each person held a stick of incense and several strings of long ingots. When they saw someone working, they used the incense to burn them. The owner, Tao Xiaochun, was burned. The 5th Branch of the Public Security Bureau sent a large number of armed police to arrest the troublemakers, including Shu Mingzheng, Ji Shunqi, and Shu Fuquan from Deda Bookbinding on Zhiyuan Road, Xia Shuangxi from Ma Hongji Bookbinding, Yin Linhai from Fuyouji Bookbinding, and workers from Hexing Box Factory, a total of thirteen people. It is hereby announced that all workers in the industry must comply and resume work within three days. Those who dare to disobey will be considered voluntarily dismissed, and each employer may recruit new workers. Be careful not to wait and see and mislead yourself.

Maintaining Order: The workers' representatives of the bookbinding industry issued a notice yesterday, stating that in this emergency, please wait patiently for a solution. If there are places where people are secretly working, only a few comrades can be sent to persuade them. Do not destroy other people's belongings. You must keep your mouths shut and not speak. This requires everyone's attention. As for the solution, we are actively working on it and will definitely have a solution to inform you. Please maintain order.

Dispute Over Sale of Guangda Steamer 162

Employees Present Reasons

Jun'an Society Submits to Prevent Sale

The Guangda Steamer of the China Merchants Bureau's Nanhua Line has been under repair at the Jiangnan Shipyard for two months. Now it has been completed. The business department staff on the ship have suffered huge losses in food, accommodation, and hotels during the suspension period. Recently, they went to the bureau to urge the start of the voyage to maintain their livelihoods. However, they suddenly heard that the bureau was taking the excuse of the Guangda being old and selling it cheaply, and someone had already contacted them. The entire ship's employees were panicked and rushed to the Jun'an Society to ask General Manager Guo to stop the sale. The reasons they put forward are: (1) The steel plate of the Guangda is the best-quality iron of Ximing Maidings, which is several times higher than that of new ships in recent times. (2) There are many ships in the bureau that are older than the Guangda and not as strong as the Guangda. (3) The ship only needs to replace a four-eyed furnace to increase speed and save five tons of coal per day. (4) It costs six to seven hundred thousand to purchase a new ship like Guangda with the current price of hardware. Now, instead of studying the repairs, we have come up with this plan of giving up eating for fear of choking, which not only causes problems for the lives of more than 100 employees on the entire ship but also causes significant losses to the bureau's business and ship prices. They asked the Jun'an Society to submit to the new General Manager to cancel the proposal to sell the Guangda. The Jun'an Society has been comforting the workers for several days, advising them not to panic and to continue to serve on the ship with peace of mind. At the same time, it submitted to the China Merchants Bureau's General Manager according to the situation reported by the workers, asking him to consider the lives of the seamen and asking General Manager Guo to personally inspect the Guangda Steamer to clarify the ship's solid advantages and not sell it at a low price, which would cause disputes.

False Accusation Against Wooden Boat Cleared 163

Lin Shicai of Xiushan, Dinghai, owned a sailing ship named Jintai Kang. On May 3 of this year, he loaded timber worth more than 17,000 yuan from the Wantai Timber Company in Fujian and transported it to the Fuheyuan Timber Company in Xiannvzhen, Yangzhou. At 5:00 pm on the 22nd, it sailed to the Damuyang waters of Zhejiang Province. The Jiangxing Steamer, which was loaded with coal, was behind the Jintai Kang sailing ship. Unexpectedly, the helmsman of the steamer neglected his duties and sailed straight towards the Jintai Kang sailing ship. The crew of the Jintai Kang shouted loudly to keep the ship away. Although the steamer heard it and urgently steered away, it was too late. The wire rope on the side of the steamer was trapped in the timber loaded on the right side of the Jintai Kang. At that time, the wind and waves were very strong, and it was impossible to untangle it. The steamer destroyed the wooden cable tied to the right side of the Jintai Kang, causing more than a thousand pieces of timber to drift away, and the spring oar was also damaged. Fortunately, it quickly anchored to avoid further collisions. Chen Ruisheng, the agent of the Jintai Kang, negotiated with the steamer and asked the steamer to tow the Jintai Kang to Dinghai. The steamer refused to tow, saying that it was too weak to tow, but said that the steamer would first go to Dinghai and then hire another steamer to tow it. Then he ordered two sailors to go to the Jintai Kang and invited Chen Ruisheng to take his ship to Dinghai to gain trust. After the agreement was reached, the steamer left first. However, after waiting until the 24th, no steamer came to tow it. Fortunately, the wooden cables were securely tied, so it was barely feasible to sail. So it raised its sails and sailed forward, and because Dafan was approaching the high tide, it was worried that the date would be missed and the business would be hindered. So instead of going to Dinghai, it sailed to Qitou and hired a small boat to send the two sailors of the Jiangxing Steamer to Dinghai, while the Jintai Kang sailed straight to the Jiangsu border and found that it had arrived at Xiannvzhen. However, after the Jiangxing Steamer arrived in Dinghai, it tried to evade compensation and falsely accused the Jintai Kang to the Dinghai Water Police Team of being a pirate ship that robbed the ship's coal. Captain Wu, without asking the truth, arrested Chen Ruisheng, who followed the ship to Dinghai, and sent the Yonggu Steamer to Qitou to detain the Jintai Kang ship. Lin had no choice but to appeal to the Zhejiang Offshore Water Police Bureau. After the bureau collected witnesses and learned the truth about the false accusation, it released Chen Ru. As for the two people who represented the Jiangxing Steamer to the case, they were ordered to post bail. The unjust grievance was reversed and praised the worthy senior official.

Solution to Doctor Registration in French Concession 164

Letter from Municipal Health Bureau to National Medical Association

After the promulgation of the draft regulations for doctor registration in the French Concession, the Shanghai National Medical Association believed that the methods were harsh and exceeded the necessary scope. The association repeatedly sent people to negotiate and requested the party and government organs to verify the matter. The association received a letter from the Municipal Health Bureau yesterday stating that the doctor registration problem in the French Concession had been resolved to a considerable extent. The original letter is summarized as follows: We have investigated the regulations for doctor registration in the French Concession and found that many of them are not appropriate. We have seriously negotiated with the French Concession and have achieved considerable results as follows: (1) Only one license is required, and the fee is two yuan. (2) Doctors and physicians who do not reside or set up clinics in the French Concession and hold official documents from this bureau do not need to register and obtain a license from the French Concession to practice medicine in the French Concession. When this bureau negotiated with the French Concession, it proposed supplementary measures to prevent unqualified doctors from mixing in, that is, each doctor and physician should take a six-inch film of the license they obtained and carry it with them when practicing medicine in the French Concession, which could be inspected by the French Concession inspectors. However, this bureau is deeply afraid that this kind of film is easy to alter, so it uses a small license that is easy to carry. Doctors and physicians who have already obtained a license can bring a two-and-a-half-inch photo of themselves to the bureau to obtain a small license. In addition to the one-dime stamp tax, there is no charge. In the future, qualified doctors and physicians who register in each session can also obtain a small license. The bureau is now rushing to make this small license, and will inform you when it is made. This is for your information. Sincerely, Shanghai National Medical Association

Page 15

New Chemical Therapy for Pulmonary Tuberculosis Discovered

Koch Discovers the Pathogen of Pulmonary Tuberculosis

Dr. Bergell Successfully Develops a Waxing Technique for Tuberculosis Bacteria

The Pathogen of Pulmonary Tuberculosis 166

Forty-nine years ago, on March 24, 1882, Dr. Robert Koch, the medical saint of Germany, presented a valuable medical paper at the Physiological Society of Berlin, Germany, entitled "The Cause of Pulmonary Tuberculosis." The purpose of the doctor's report was that pulmonary tuberculosis (i.e., consumption) is a special infectious disease and not a genetic disease, and he cited various examples to prove it (such as the culture, staining, and animal experiments of tuberculosis bacteria). Since then, in the history of pulmonary tuberculosis research for the past 3,000 years, a special splendor has been opened, and the pathogen of pulmonary tuberculosis has been identified, and a clear standard for the diagnosis of pulmonary tuberculosis has been obtained.

The tuberculosis bacteria is a microscopic bacteria, and its shape is extremely small. If one gram is weighed, the number is more than 3.5 million. Its reproduction is extremely alarming, destroying the body tissue to form the most terrible tuberculosis symptoms. If this bacteria is discharged from the human body, it cannot reproduce at all, and can only maintain its survival. However, once there is an opportunity to invade the human body, it will occupy the tender lungs as its base camp and display its terrible power. Alas, the greatest enemy of mankind is pulmonary tuberculosis, which is not to be feared.

The Structure of Tuberculosis Bacteria 167

In the past, the general medical community did not understand the special structure of tuberculosis bacteria, thinking that all bacteria can be reduced by using disinfection agents internally or by injection, such as the injection of Salvarsan for syphilis. After Dr. Bergell's painstaking research, he published that pulmonary tuberculosis has a special defense force that can resist all external drug attacks. The tuberculosis bacteria body is composed of an inner membrane of neutral fat and an outer membrane of acid-fast wax. If it is not possible to destroy the waxy defense line and remove its fatty armor, there is no way to capture the tuberculosis bacteria and put it to death. Moreover, when tuberculosis bacteria invades a local part of the human body, its surroundings are eroded to form a strong nodule to block the passage of blood flow, so that an injected or internally taken disinfectant can not cross the Lei Chi step, just like a specially martial law zone. Since the drug power cannot contact the affected part, even if the whole body is drowned in a drug pool, it cannot hurt the tuberculosis bacteria. Therefore, the only combat strategy to eliminate tuberculosis bacteria must have at least the following two preconditions: (1) Any drug that can destroy the nodules and directly reach the affected part.

(2) It can also strip and dissolve the waxy and fatty inner and outer membranes.

Only in this way can the merit of breaking through the barriers be achieved. Otherwise, it is like scratching an itch through a shoe. The tuberculosis bacteria will secretly laugh at people's inability to harm it under these two guarantees.

The inventor of tuberculosis bacteria, the German medical saint Dr. Koch

Successful Waxing of Tuberculosis Bacteria 168

Since Dr. Koch discovered that tuberculosis bacteria is the pathogen of pulmonary tuberculosis (i.e., consumption), tuberculosis scholars in the East and West have competed to study and want to find a wonderful way to kill this bacteria, but the results have all failed because they do not know the profound theory that tuberculosis bacteria can secrete a waxy substance to surround its body to resist external force invasion. There have been those such as Hamosehali who discovered that using a caustic potash liquid of 5% or less can remove the acid-fast wax of tuberculosis bacteria. Later, Mr. Mo used chlorine gas to remove the acid-fast wax. However, this waxing method can only be applied to the staining method in microscopic examination, because its medicinal properties are extremely toxic and cannot be used for the human body.

In recent years, there have been occasional unexpected results in applying chaulmoogra oil to leprosy, because leprosy bacteria and tuberculosis bacteria are acid-fast bacteria of the same nature, and chaulmoogra oil can have a waxing effect and has a sterilizing power more than a hundred times that of carbolic acid. As a result, the general scholars have aroused fanatical attention and tried to apply chaulmoogra oil to patients with tuberculosis in the hope of a result, and various chemical methods have been proposed. The main components of chaulmoogra oil are tested on patients with tuberculosis, and it is also hoped that a considerable effect can be obtained, but it is limited to the skin and superficial tuberculosis that can have a good effect, while the deep-seated organ tuberculosis such as the lungs, liver, and kidneys still cannot have any effect.

Therefore, Dr. Bergell, the great teacher of the world's tuberculosis sufferers, has gone a step further to collect various drugs of animal, plant, and mineral origin and study them painstakingly in the hope of obtaining a waxing effect and a peaceful and non-toxic medicinal property. For decades, he did not know how much brainpower he had exhausted and how much effort he had put into seeking the most reasonable and effective chemical agent. Finally, he discovered that a certain effective component in the compressed juice of the interintestinal mesenteric gland of a special animal has a strong waxing effect on tuberculosis bacteria. Then, he applied this new component to tuberculosis bacteria, and the result was completely dewaxed. Since then, the claim that the acid resistance of tuberculosis bacteria cannot be removed by human work, which was regarded by doctors in the East and West in the past, has been completely overturned. It is a new dawn in the treatment of pulmonary tuberculosis, a great question in the medical world throughout the ages.

Chemical Treatment of Pulmonary Tuberculosis 169

The cause of pulmonary tuberculosis (i.e., consumption) is the tubercle bacillus. Once this bacterium enters the human body, it forms nodules at that site, blocking the flow of blood. Furthermore, the tubercle bacillus secretes an acid-resistant waxy substance that surrounds it, protecting it from the intrusion of external medicinal forces. Therefore, although various bactericidal drugs are taken internally or injected, they ultimately fail to reach the actual body of the pathogen. The natural therapies, symptomatic treatments, physical therapies, serum therapies, drug therapies, and all other treatments commonly used by medical practitioners in the past have not been completely successful. The saying that there is no cure for pulmonary tuberculosis has persisted throughout the ages because people were unaware of this profound and intricate scientific principle. Consequently, modern tuberculosis researchers, based on the aforementioned scientific theory, have continued to conduct tireless research, and as a result, have successfully developed a chemical agent that eradicates pulmonary tuberculosis bacilli, called SANOSIN. This drug was developed based on the latest medical theories of Dr. Koch of Germany, the discoverer of the pulmonary tuberculosis bacillus, and Dr. Bengel of Germany, the inventor of the dewaxing technique for the pulmonary tuberculosis bacillus. According to experimental reports from various pulmonary disease sanatoriums in Germany, Switzerland, and other countries, this drug has the effect of penetrating pulmonary nodules and dissolving waxy substances, while also possessing bactericidal power, enabling a complete cure for stages one, two, and three of pulmonary tuberculosis. It is indeed effective in every case. In China, the Central Hygiene Laboratory of the National Government has tested the drug and confirmed that it is harmless and non-toxic, with absolutely no side effects. A brief summary of its therapeutic effects is provided below:

(1) In experiments conducted in test tubes, the medicinal effects of Sanosin cause the tubercle bacilli to disappear within one minute. After three minutes, the acid resistance is lost, and the pulmonary tubercle bacilli are completely eradicated without exception.

(2) Animal experiments have revealed that Sanosin can penetrate tuberculous foci. Examination of the tubercle bacilli latent within the foci reveals that they have lost their acid resistance, which sufficiently proves the complete dissolution of the waxy substance.

(3) If a patient takes Sanosin internally for about a week, immediate improvements such as sputum dilution and reduction of body temperature will be observed.

(4) Continuing to take Sanosin internally for thirty to sixty days or more will visibly lead to increased body weight, stimulated appetite, and gradual alleviation of all symptoms, ultimately achieving the remarkable effect of restoring health.

A Sanosin experimental report and a pulmonary disease treatment guide are available upon request by mail.

Relief Committee Presents Plaque to Du Ancestral Hall 173

Du Yuesheng, a prominent gentleman of Shanghai and a respected member of the local community, is known for his charitable deeds. During the recent renovation of his ancestral hall, various organizations and entities, including President Chiang of the National Government, presented plaques to celebrate the occasion. Chairman Xu Shiying of the Central Relief Committee, recognizing Du's tireless efforts in soliciting donations for disaster relief in various provinces and his generous contributions to alleviate the suffering of disaster victims, specially commissioned a plaque bearing the inscription "Accumulating Virtue Brings Lasting Blessings." It is said that Mr. Xu personally composed the calligraphy, which is elegant and meticulously crafted. Yesterday, Jin Guanfu, Deputy Secretary-General of the Relief Committee stationed in Shanghai, and Mr. Qi Junqing, along with a military band and a decorative pavilion, represented the committee in delivering the plaque to the Du residence. Mr. Qi also invited the Political Department of the French Concession Police and patrol detectives to provide security along the route. Furthermore, philanthropist Zhu Qinglan presented a plaque inscribed with "Universally Known Benevolent Gate," which was also delivered by Jin and Qi. Mr. Du personally received the gifts with repeated expressions of humility. Observers commented that this honor was a result of Mr. Du's widespread charitable acts.

Grand Prayer at the Wusong Jisheng Branch 174

The Wusong branch of the Chinese Jisheng Society, fearing that the people would suffer from disasters during this time of rampant white-flag calamities, has launched a three-day grand peace prayer ceremony, scheduled from the 5th to the 7th of this month, to invoke divine harmony and avert calamities. Wusong Charity Organizations Hold Meeting Regarding Floating Corpses 175

Scheduled to Send Representatives to Petition the Court

The Wusong Jide Hall is a charitable organization that handles the unidentified floating corpses recovered from the sea and river by the Lifesaving Bureau, as well as corpses found dead on the streets. The hall takes photographs, examines the bodies for any identifying items, and fills out a corpse identification form. If there are any injuries, the local security officer is immediately instructed to report them to the judicial authorities for investigation. If there are no injuries, the hall prepares a coffin, shrouds the body, and transports it to a charitable cemetery, then advertises for relatives to claim the body. This procedure was previously approved by the former Baoshan County government and has been implemented for many years. Recently, the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau, emphasizing the importance of human life, instructed the Seventh District Office of Wusong that all unidentified floating corpses recovered by the Lifesaving Bureau, regardless of whether they have injuries, must be reported to the local court for investigation before being claimed. However, since the implementation of this new procedure, each floating corpse discovered has required the security officer to report to the court and the prosecutor to travel to Wusong for the inquest, which is a cumbersome process, especially considering the distance between Wusong and Shanghai. This delay often causes the corpse to be left unattended for one or two days or more. Recognizing that the hot weather will cause the floating corpses to decompose quickly if left unattended for too long, emitting foul odors and posing a threat to public health, Jide Hall convened a joint temporary meeting of its board of directors, the Lifesaving Bureau, and personnel from the Municipal Affairs Committee Office yesterday at 1:00 p.m. at the Lifesaving Bureau to discuss solutions. It was generally agreed that the lives of the deceased are certainly important, but the health of all residents in the town should also be considered. After extensive discussion, it was decided that Municipal Affairs Committee member Liu Ziwen and Lifesaving Bureau standing director Gu Danchao would draft a summary, and Zhang Qingshi, Yin Zhenfu, Gu Danchao, and Liu Ziwen would be elected as representatives, along with lawyer Yuan Xilian, to visit the local court and the Social Affairs, Public Security, and Health Bureaus at 9:00 a.m. on the 6th to discuss a satisfactory solution.

Chinese Again Expelled by Japanese 176

Japan treats the expulsion and prohibition of Chinese laborers as a common practice. Recently, Shanghai residents Wei Xiaopin, Lin Zufeng, Guo Yigui, and Xue Jiachen were all traveling to Japan as kimono merchants. However, upon arriving in Kobe, the Japanese Maritime Police refused to allow them to disembark and forced them back onto the original ship to return to Shanghai. Furthermore, Hua Shicai and Qian Liangkun were two students traveling to Kyoto, Japan, to study, accompanied by a political science university student named Ma. However, upon arriving in Kobe, the Japanese police claimed that Hua and Qian's clothing did not resemble that of students and refused to allow them to disembark, forcing them back onto the Nagasaki Maru to return home. They arrived in Shanghai yesterday. The travel expenses incurred by all of the above individuals during this time of heightened anti-Chinese sentiment were substantial.

At 6:30 a.m. yesterday, the Nisshin Company's Yangtze River steamer Nanyo Maru, departing from Shanghai to Hankou, was passing the Waitan Bridge when it collided with a cargo barge due to the swift current. Ms. Liu Manqing Arrives in Shanghai Today 178

Due to the repeated conflicts that have arisen in Kangzang in recent years, although the Central Government has dispatched personnel to mediate, newspapers have recently reported that Tibetan troops are still attacking Xikang. The Dalai Lama consistently obeys the British, essentially making it a British territory. The National Government, concerned about the border residents, urgently desires to understand the truth in order to respond appropriately and prevent the transfer of the vast Tibetan territory to British hands. Therefore, it has specially appointed National Government official Ms. Liu Manqing as a special envoy to Tibet. After receiving her orders, Ms. Liu showed no hesitation and, without bringing any attendants, bravely entered Tibet alone to convey the Central Government's intentions. A weak woman venturing thousands of miles into remote and barren regions is truly a rare female hero. Therefore, newspapers at home and abroad have reported on her actions. Many gentlemen and women in Shanghai admire Ms. Liu's ambition. It is learned that Ms. Liu will arrive in Shanghai today. Party affairs commissioners Ge Sang Zeren, writer Yang Zhonghua, Jiang Weixin, military strategist Xue Fengxian, radio expert Pan Ruyan, educator Liu Manyun, and a group of more than ten others, specially sent by the Xikang party to bid farewell, will take the opportunity to visit and express concern for the comrades in the border region, investigate cultural enterprises, and visit Shen Xin Times, Great News, Culture, and China pictorials. They plan to stay for about four days and then return to Beijing. On Saturday, she will give a major public lecture in Shanghai about her experiences traveling to Tibet. Her travelogue has been submitted to the Commercial Press for publication.

World Women's Temperance Convention Opens Today 179

The World Women's Temperance Union, an organization composed of women's temperance groups from fifty-one countries, is dedicated to prohibiting tobacco, alcohol, gambling, and vice, and promoting international peace. It holds a convention every three years. The previous 13th convention was held in Lausanne, Switzerland. The Chinese representative was the wife of Mr. Zhao Quan, the Chinese representative to the League of Nations. This year's convention is being held at the Toronto Royal Hotel in Canada. Ms. Liu Wang Liming was originally appointed as the Chinese representative, but she was unable to attend due to the domestic temperance society being busy and her family affairs. Therefore, the wife of the Chinese ambassador to the United States, Wu Chaoshu, and Ms. Chen Weikun, the former president of the Shantou Temperance Branch who is currently studying in the United States, have been specially invited as representatives.

Subsidies for Confiscated Diseased Livestock 180

Regulations Revised

The Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau announced the following notice: To eliminate the mixing and sale of meat from animals infected with epidemic diseases and maintain public health regarding meat consumption, subsidies were previously approved to be disbursed to merchants as compensation for their losses, and the subsidy amounts were specified in the operating regulations for rendering plants for diseased livestock. With the approval of the Municipal Government, the subsidy standards for diseased livestock have been revised and are listed below for your information. The subsidy amounts for diseased livestock are as follows: Diseased pigs (regardless of pre-slaughter or post-slaughter): $1 per head; Pre-slaughter large yellow cattle: $6 per head; Pre-slaughter large water buffalo: $5 per head; Pre-slaughter small cattle: $3 per head; Post-slaughter large yellow cattle: $8 per head; Post-slaughter large water buffalo: $7 per head; Post-slaughter small cattle: $5 per head; Sheep (regardless of pre-slaughter or post-slaughter): $0.80 per head; Goats (regardless of pre-slaughter or post-slaughter): $0.70 per head; Horses and donkeys (regardless of size): $5 per head. Hu Hongji, Director, June 3, 1931.

Dong Tangjia Lane Nursery Achieves Excellent Results 182

The Dong Tangjia Lane Nursery inside the Great South Gate was founded in the 48th year of the Kangxi reign of the Qing Dynasty and has existed for 222 years, making it a pioneer among Shanghai's charitable institutions. Recently, Mr. Huang Xingjie took over its management. Mr. Huang is highly enthusiastic and has made every effort to reorganize the nursery. Our reporter made a special visit and observed that each child was dressed in new, clean clothing, and all had rosy lips and fair skin and were very plump and lively. Some were asleep in beds, while others were being breastfed by their wet nurses. Each of them was adorable. The wet nurses cared for the infants as if they were their own, with exceptional affection. Even the Shanghai infant competition held previously was not as grand as this. Inside the nursery, only laughter was heard, and not a single cry. This demonstrates the excellent results achieved by the nursery in caring for the infants.
